[1;36m5[0m | # Constraint [1;36m2[0m: No overlap between pieces
def [1;35mrectangles_overlap[0m[1m([0mx1, y1, w1, h1, x2, y2, w2, h2[1m)[0m:
    [32m"""Check if two rectangles overlap"""[0m
    # No overlap if one rectangle is completely to the left, right, above, or below the other
    return not [1m([0mx1 + w1 [1m<[0m[39m= x2 or x2 + w2 <= x1 or y1 + h1 <= y2 or y2 + h2 <= y1[0m[1;39m)[0m

[1;36m6[0m[39m | # Objective: Minimize the maximum length used[0m
[39m# We'll implement this through binary search[0m

[39mdef [0m[1;35msolve_with_length_limit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmax_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m
[39m    [0m[32m"""Try to solve with a given maximum length constraint"""[0m

[39m    if solvable:[0m

[39m    [0m[1;35msolver.delete[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m    return solvable, result_model, length_violations[0m

[39m        best_length = mid_length[0m
[39m        best_model = model[0m
[39m        max_length = mid_length - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m  # Try to find shorter[0m
[39m    else:[0m
[39m        [0m[1;35mprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mf"✗ No solution with length [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mmid_length[0m[1;39m}[0m[39mft [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m{[0m[39mviolations[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m violations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m"[0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m        min_length = mid_length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m  # Need longer[0m

[39mif best_model is [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m:[0m

[1;36m5[0m | # Constraint [1;36m2[0m: No overlap between pieces
def [1;35mrectangles_overlap[0m[1m([0mx1, y1, w1, h1, x2, y2, w2, h2[1m)[0m:
    [32m"""Check if two rectangles overlap"""[0m
    # No overlap if one rectangle is completely to the left, right, above, or below the other
    return not [1m([0mx1 + w1 [1m<[0m[39m= x2 or x2 + w2 <= x1 or y1 + h1 <= y2 or y2 + h2 <= y1[0m[1;39m)[0m

[39m# For each pair of placement variables, if both are true, their rectangles must not overlap[0m
[39moverlap_constraints = [0m[1;36m0[0m
[39mfor i, var1 in [0m[1;35menumerate[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mpiece_placement_vars.keys[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m

[39m        if i >= j:  # Avoid duplicate constraints and self-comparison[0m
[39m            continue[0m

[39m        info2 = piece_placement_vars[0m
[39m        [0m
[39m        # Check if these two placements would overlap[0m
[39m        if [0m[1;35mrectangles_overlap[0m[1;39m([0m[39minfo1[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'x'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, info1[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'y'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, info1[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'width'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, info1[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'height'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m

[39m            overlap_constraints += [0m[1;36m1[0m

[1;36m2[0m | # Create variable mapping and formula

var_mapping = [1m{[0m[1m}[0m
var_count = [1;36m1[0m

def [1;35mcreate_var[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m:
    global var_count
    var_mapping = var_count
    var_count += [1;36m1[0m
    return var_mapping

# For minimization, we'll use binary search on the maximum length used
# Start with a reasonable upper bound
max_length_bound = [1;35msum[0m[1m([0mw * h for w, h, q in pieces[1m)[0m [35m/[0m[35m/[0m ROLL_WIDTH + [1;36m1[0m
max_length_bound = [1;35mmin[0m[1m([0mmax_length_bound, ROLL_LENGTH[1m)[0m

[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Maximum length search bound: [1m{[0mmax_length_bound[1m}[0mft"[1m)[0m
[1;36m3[0m | # Simplified direct approach: enumerate valid placements
# For each piece, find all valid positions [1m([0mconsidering rotation[1m)[0m

def [1;35mget_valid_placements[0m[1m([0mwidth, height, roll_width, roll_length[1m)[0m:
    [32m"""Get all valid [0m[32m([0m[32mx, y, rotated[0m[32m)[0m[32m placements for a piece"""[0m
    placements = [1m[[0m[1m][0m
    
    # Try without rotation
    for x in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mroll_width - width + [1;36m1[0m[1m)[0m:
        for y in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mroll_length - height + [1;36m1[0m[1m)[0m:
            [1;35mplacements.append[0m[1m([0m[1m([0mx, y, [3;91mFalse[0m, width, height[1m)[0m[1m)[0m
    
    # Try with [1;36m90[0m° rotation [1m([0mif different dimensions[1m)[0m
    if width != height:
        for x in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mroll_width - height + [1;36m1[0m[1m)[0m:
            for y in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mroll_length - width + [1;36m1[0m[1m)[0m:
                [1;35mplacements.append[0m[1m([0m[1m([0mx, y, [3;92mTrue[0m, height, width[1m)[0m[1m)[0m
    
    return placements

# Create variables for each valid placement of each piece
piece_placement_vars = [1m{[0m[1m}[0m
pieces_info = [1m[[0m[1m][0m

for piece_id, [1m([0mbase_w, base_h, quantity[1m)[0m in [1;35menumerate[0m[1m([0mpieces[1m)[0m:
    for instance in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mquantity[1m)[0m:

        # Get all valid placements for this piece

        # Create a variable for each valid placement
        placement_vars = [1m[[0m[1m][0m
        for i, [1m([0mx, y, rotated, w, h[1m)[0m in [1;35menumerate[0m[1m([0mvalid_placements[1m)[0m:

            var_id = [1;35mcreate_var[0m[1m([0mvar_name[1m)[0m
            [1;35mplacement_vars.append[0m[1m([0mvar_id[1m)[0m
            
            # Store placement info
            piece_placement_vars = [1m{[0m
                [32m'piece_key'[0m: piece_key,
                [32m'piece_id'[0m: piece_id,
                [32m'instance'[0m: instance,
                [32m'x'[0m: x, [32m'y'[0m: y, 
                [32m'rotated'[0m: rotated,
                [32m'width'[0m: w, [32m'height'[0m: h,
                [32m'placement_id'[0m: i
            [1m}[0m
        
        [1;35mpieces_info.append[0m[1m([0m[1m{[0m
            [32m'key'[0m: piece_key,
            [32m'id'[0m: piece_id,
            [32m'instance'[0m: instance,
            [32m'base_width'[0m: base_w,
            [32m'base_height'[0m: base_h,
            [32m'placement_vars'[0m: placement_vars,
            [32m'num_placements'[0m: [1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mvalid_placements[1m)[0m
        [1m}[0m[1m)[0m

total_placements = [1;35msum[0m[1m([0m[1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mp[1m[[0m[32m'placement_vars'[0m[1m][0m[1m)[0m for p in pieces_info[1m)[0m

[1;36m4[0m | # Constraint [1;36m1[0m: Each piece must have exactly one placement

    # Exactly one placement for each piece
    for clause in [1;35mexactly_one[0m[1m([0mpiece[1m[[0m[32m'placement_vars'[0m[1m][0m[1m)[0m:
        [1;35mformula.append[0m[1m([0mclause[1m)[0m

[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Added placement uniqueness constraints"[0m[1m)[0m
[1;36m5[0m | # Constraint [1;36m2[0m: No overlap between pieces
def [1;35mrectangles_overlap[0m[1m([0mx1, y1, w1, h1, x2, y2, w2, h2[1m)[0m:
    [32m"""Check if two rectangles overlap"""[0m
    # No overlap if one rectangle is completely to the left, right, above, or below the other
    return not [1m([0mx1 + w1 [1m<[0m[39m= x2 or x2 + w2 <= x1 or y1 + h1 <= y2 or y2 + h2 <= y1[0m[1;39m)[0m

[39m# For each pair of placement variables, if both are true, their rectangles must not overlap[0m
[39moverlap_constraints = [0m[1;36m0[0m
[39mfor i, var1 in [0m[1;35menumerate[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mpiece_placement_vars.keys[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m

[39m    for j, var2 in [0m[1;35menumerate[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mpiece_placement_vars.keys[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m
[39m        if i >= j:  # Avoid duplicate constraints and self-comparison[0m
[39m            continue[0m
[39m            [0m
[39m        info2 = piece_placement_vars[0m
[39m        [0m
[39m        # Check if these two placements would overlap[0m
[39m        if [0m[1;35mrectangles_overlap[0m[1;39m([0m[39minfo1[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'x'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, info1[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'y'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, info1[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'width'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, info1[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'height'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m
[39m                            info2[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'x'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, info2[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'y'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, info2[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'width'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, info2[0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'height'[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m
[39m            # Add constraint: not both can be true[0m
[39m            [0m[1;35mformula.append[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m[[0m[39m-var1, -var2[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m            overlap_constraints += [0m[1;36m1[0m

[1;35mprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mf"Added [0m[1;39m{[0m[39moverlap_constraints[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m non-overlap constraints"[0m[1;39m)[0m
[1;36m6[0m[39m | # Objective: Minimize the maximum length used[0m
[39m# We'll implement this through binary search[0m

[39mdef [0m[1;35msolve_with_length_limit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmax_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m
[39m    [0m[32m"""Try to solve with a given maximum length constraint"""[0m
[39m    temp_formula = [0m[1;35mCNF[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m    [0m
[39m    # Add all existing constraints[0m
[39m    for clause in formula:[0m
[39m        [0m[1;35mtemp_formula.append[0m[1;39m([0m[39mclause[0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m    [0m
[39m    # Add length constraint: no piece can extend beyond max_length[0m

[39m    for var_id, placement_data in [0m[1;35mpiece_placement_vars.items[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m

[39m        if max_y > max_length:[0m
[39m            # This placement violates the length constraint[0m
[39m            [0m[1;35mtemp_formula.append[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m[[0m[39m-var_id[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m

[39m    [0m[1;35msolver.append_formula[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtemp_formula[0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m    solvable = [0m[1;35msolver.solve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m

[39m    if solvable:[0m
[39m        result_model = [0m[1;35msolver.get_model[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m    [0m
[39m    [0m[1;35msolver.delete[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m    return solvable, result_model, length_violations[0m

[39mmax_length = ROLL_LENGTH[0m
[39mbest_length = [0m[3;35mNone[0m

[39mwhile min_length <= max_length:[0m
[39m    mid_length = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmin_length + max_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m
[39m    [0m[1;35mprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mf"Trying length limit: [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mmid_length[0m[1;39m}[0m[39mft"[0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m    [0m
[39m    solvable, model, violations = [0m[1;35msolve_with_length_limit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmid_length[0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m    [0m
[39m    if solvable:[0m

[39m        best_model = model[0m
[39m        max_length = mid_length - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m  # Try to find shorter[0m
[39m    else:[0m
[39m        [0m[1;35mprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mf"✗ No solution with length [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mmid_length[0m[1;39m}[0m[39mft [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m{[0m[39mviolations[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m violations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m"[0m[1;39m)[0m
[39m        min_length = mid_length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m  # Need longer[0m

[39mif best_model is [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m:[0m

[39melse:[0m
[39m    [0m[1;35mprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mf"\nOptimal solution found with length: [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mbest_length[0m[1;39m}[0m[39mft"[0m[1;39m)[0m
[1;36m7[0m[39m | # Process and display the optimal solution[0m
[39mif best_model is not [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m:[0m
[39m    # Extract piece placements from the model[0m

┌───────────────────┐
│ PROBLEM STATEMENT │
└───────────────────┘
A carpet installer needs to efficiently cut rectangular carpet pieces from a single standard-sized roll, minimizing waste.

### Given:

- 1 standard carpet roll measuring 12ft × 50ft
- Need to cut the following rectangular pieces:
  1. 6ft × 8ft (quantity: 1)
  2. 4ft × 5ft (quantity: 1)
  3. 5ft × 7ft (quantity: 1)
  4. 8ft × 10ft (quantity: 1)

### Constraints:

1. All pieces must be placed without overlap
2. Pieces can optionally be rotated 90 degrees
3. All pieces must fit within the roll dimensions

### Objective:

Minimize the total length of carpet roll used



┌─────────────┐
│ FINAL MODEL │
└─────────────┘
0 | from pysat.formula import CNF
from pysat.solvers import Glucose3
from pysat.card import *

# PARAMETER VERIFICATION - Carpet cutting problem
# Roll dimensions: 12ft × 50ft
# Pieces: 6×8, 4×5, 5×7, 8×10 (all quantity 1)

ROLL_WIDTH = 12
ROLL_LENGTH = 50
pieces = [(6, 8), (4, 5), (5, 7), (8, 10)]

print(f"Roll: {ROLL_WIDTH}×{ROLL_LENGTH}, Pieces: {pieces}")

# Create SAT model
formula = CNF()
var_count = 1

def next_var():
    global var_count
    var_count += 1
    return var_count - 1

# For each piece, create variables for all valid positions (with/without rotation)
piece_vars = []
piece_positions = []

for p_idx, (w, h) in enumerate(pieces):
    positions = []
    vars_for_piece = []
    
    # Without rotation
    for x in range(ROLL_WIDTH - w + 1):
        for y in range(ROLL_LENGTH - h + 1):
            var_id = next_var()
            positions.append((x, y, x+w, y+h, False))  # x, y, x_end, y_end, rotated
            vars_for_piece.append(var_id)
    
    # With rotation (if different dimensions)
    if w != h:
        for x in range(ROLL_WIDTH - h + 1):
            for y in range(ROLL_LENGTH - w + 1):
                var_id = next_var()
                positions.append((x, y, x+h, y+w, True))  # rotated: h becomes width, w becomes height
                vars_for_piece.append(var_id)
    
    piece_vars.append(vars_for_piece)
    piece_positions.append(positions)

print(f"Created {sum(len(pv) for pv in piece_vars)} placement variables")
1 | # Constraint 1: Each piece must be placed exactly once
for vars_for_piece in piece_vars:
    for clause in exactly_one(vars_for_piece):
        formula.append(clause)

# Constraint 2: No overlaps
for p1_idx in range(len(pieces)):
    for p2_idx in range(p1_idx + 1, len(pieces)):
        for v1_idx, var1 in enumerate(piece_vars[p1_idx]):
            pos1 = piece_positions[p1_idx][v1_idx]
            x1, y1, x1_end, y1_end, _ = pos1
            
            for v2_idx, var2 in enumerate(piece_vars[p2_idx]):
                pos2 = piece_positions[p2_idx][v2_idx]
                x2, y2, x2_end, y2_end, _ = pos2
                
                # Check if rectangles overlap
                if not (x1_end <= x2 or x2_end <= x1 or y1_end <= y2 or y2_end <= y1):
                    # They overlap, so both can't be true
                    formula.append([-var1, -var2])

print("Added constraints")
2 | # Binary search for minimum length
def solve_with_max_length(max_len):
    temp_formula = CNF()
    for clause in formula:
        temp_formula.append(clause)
    
    # Add length constraints
    for p_idx in range(len(pieces)):
        for v_idx, var_id in enumerate(piece_vars[p_idx]):
            _, _, _, y_end, _ = piece_positions[p_idx][v_idx]
            if y_end > max_len:
                temp_formula.append([-var_id])
    
    solver = Glucose3()
    solver.append_formula(temp_formula)
    result = solver.solve()
    model = solver.get_model() if result else None
    solver.delete()
    return result, model

# Binary search
left, right = 1, ROLL_LENGTH
best_length = None
best_solution = None

while left <= right:
    mid = (left + right) // 2
    solvable, model = solve_with_max_length(mid)
    
    if solvable:
        best_length = mid
        best_solution = model
        right = mid - 1
        print(f"✓ Solution found with length {mid}")
    else:
        left = mid + 1
        print(f"✗ No solution with length {mid}")

print(f"
Optimal length: {best_length}ft")
3 | # Process solution
if best_solution:
    solution_data = {}
    actual_max_y = 0
    
    for p_idx in range(len(pieces)):
        w_orig, h_orig = pieces[p_idx]
        
        for v_idx, var_id in enumerate(piece_vars[p_idx]):
            if var_id in best_solution:  # This placement is chosen
                x, y, x_end, y_end, rotated = piece_positions[p_idx][v_idx]
                actual_max_y = max(actual_max_y, y_end)
                
                placement_width = x_end - x
                placement_height = y_end - y
                
                solution_data[f"piece_{p_idx}"] = {
                    'piece_id': p_idx,
                    'x': x, 'y': y,
                    'width': placement_width,
                    'height': placement_height,
                    'rotated': rotated,
                    'original_dims': f"{w_orig}×{h_orig}"
                }
                break
    
    print(f"
=== OPTIMAL CARPET CUTTING SOLUTION ===")
    print(f"Minimum length needed: {actual_max_y}ft")
    print(f"Roll waste saved: {(ROLL_LENGTH - actual_max_y) * ROLL_WIDTH}ft²")
    
    for key, data in solution_data.items():
        piece_num = data['piece_id'] + 1
        rot_text = " (rotated 90°)" if data['rotated'] else ""
        print(f"  Piece {piece_num} ({data['original_dims']}): ({data['x']},{data['y']}) - {data['width']}×{data['height']}{rot_text}")
    
    export_solution({
        "satisfiable": True,
        "optimal_length": actual_max_y,
        "area_saved": (ROLL_LENGTH - actual_max_y) * ROLL_WIDTH,
        "placements": solution_data
    })
else:
    export_solution({
        "satisfiable": False,
        "message": "No solution found"
    })

## Problem Analysis

The problem requires cutting 4 rectangular pieces from a 12ft × 50ft carpet roll:
1. 6ft × 8ft (quantity: 1)
2. 4ft × 5ft (quantity: 1) 
3. 5ft × 7ft (quantity: 1)
4. 8ft × 10ft (quantity: 1)

The constraints are:
1. All pieces must be placed without overlap
2. Pieces can optionally be rotated 90 degrees
3. All pieces must fit within the roll dimensions (12ft width × 50ft length)
4. Minimize the total length of carpet roll used

## Solution Analysis

The solution claims to find an optimal arrangement using 18ft of length with the following placements:
- Piece 1 (6×8): positioned at (5,10) with dimensions 6×8 (not rotated)
